The letter "Z" was not supposed to be any symbol. As the Russian hold military exercise i was classic like every other military exercises in the world. There are troops who defend and troops who attack so one side play defenders and other attackers. To make difference vehicles need a mark, of course. This was the big letter "Z", meaning "zapad" or west and was meant as NATO forces approaching of course from the western direction. Some days after as the attack on the Ukraine was prepared they had to mark all vehicles with "Z" to make difference between them and Ukrainian. As the raid should last not more as one or two weeks letter "Z" in this case would be not so much important. But as the war continue it became symbol and Russian had to find the meaning for it trying to boost morale as the war was not so successfully for Russians.  Similarly to this there was the letter "V", meaning NATO troops approaching from the east, meaning Turkey but since all attention was concentrated around Kyiv the letter "Z" was far more in focus. At the end Russians had to use latin letter to find out a meaning to boost morale and nobody really ask what is this mean and why is not on cirillic but latin

In general, there is another theory of the origin of z and v symbol, I don't know know true they are. Before the war start, troops were pulled for exercises, so if I understand correct, troops must be divided into two teams, for example east(in russian vostok) and west (zapad). In cyrillic alphabet letters z(–ó) and v(–í) quite similar, so the can be confused, so they used Latin analogue. And when war started they were too busy to delete them

This symbols chosen because they easy to defy in optical visors. Because russian army has to use cellular phones to coordinate, they have no radio sets or Glonass devices. First one - Z [zet] - for donetsk-luhansk direction - is fulfilled square, it is used on documents in Russia, when you have write something and do not want anybody to add more text right after yours. So it is visually a square. Second one - V [vi] - moving from Belarus - is a triangle shape, easy to defy, easy in pronouncing. Third one - O [ou] - support, rotation forces - circle shaped.
This symbols chosen because they easy to defy in optical visors. Because russian army has to use cellular phones to coordinate, they have no radio sets or Glonass devices. First one - Z [zet] - for donetsk-luhansk direction - is fulfilled square, it is used on documents in Russia, when you have write something and do not want anybody to add more text right after yours. So it is visually a square. Second one - V [vi] - moving from Belarus - is a triangle shape, easy to defy, easy in pronouncing. Third one - O [ou] - support, rotation forces - circle shaped.

World War III Has Begun; How It Unfolds Depends on Us We think of the Russia-Ukraine war as a local conflict, but it is much more than that; it is a global war on multiple fronts. The war is not only a military conflict; it is also an economic war of attrition. With skyrocketing gas prices and shortage of staples, people all over the world are feeling the consequences of the war This war is transforming the entire modus operandi of humanity. Since the dawn of time, we have been accustomed to living by the motto, ‚Äúsurvival of the fittest.‚Äù By and large, the rule was that the strong determined the rules, and the rules were often abusive toward the weak. Now, it seems like a new mindset has set in: Wanting something and being strong enough to take it does not mean that the world will accept it. The war, therefore, is being fought on the inside no less, and perhaps more than on the outside. Our very makeup is changing from abusive to cooperative, from narcissistic to altruistic. It hurts, and it will not happen without a struggle, but it is irreversible. This is the path of our evolution toward the purpose of our creation‚Äîto encompass within us all of creation. To do that, we must come to care for it, just as a mother encompasses her child through her maternal love. The struggle to transition from our current uncaring and mean approach to all creations but ourselves, into wise and compassionate beings is called ‚Äúthe war of Gog and Magog‚Äù or Armageddon. Since the war is about our inner makeup, we can fight it within us. If we object to struggling with ourselves over who will rule‚Äîthe ego or love‚Äîthe physical reality will force us to choose love nonetheless. However, it will do so by hurting us in a very physical way. The war in Eastern Europe is nothing compared to what we might have to endure if we resist the process. The horrific descriptions of our sages and prophets hint at it, and we would not want to live through it. Alternatively, we can fight this war within us without firing a single bullet. The choice is in our hands. All we need is to continue in the same direction that nature is already leading us: toward connection. One plausible theory is that the symbols relate to the Russian military districts: Z - Zavod (West), forces from the western military district who predominantly fight at the southern (from Mykolaiv to Mariupol and Donbass) and and eastern flank (Donbass up to Sumy). V - Vostok (East), forces from the eastern military district who were deployed in the north (Kyiv). It looks like the VDV troops adopted it. O - Central and possibly northern military  district, who fought at Sumy down to Chernihiv. The letter might just symbolise the "center" graphically rather than stand for any particular word.  Examples:  -4th Guards Tank Division is an elite western military district unit. Used Z, had significant losses between Kharkiv and Sumy. -90th Tank Division is part of the central military district. Their units were seen carring the O symbol, rushing from Chernihiv and Sumy to Brovary where they got beaten up. -18th Guards Assault Aviation Regiment is stationed in the far east. Like all units fielded north-west of Kyiv they used the V symbol and got smashed at Irpin.
